#Amyzonis' AN overhaul of formables

country_decisions = {

#### Post-Discovery Formables
# Lusitania	
AN_lusitania_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_lusitania_flag }
		LSA = { exists = no }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
				tag = SPA
				tag = SPI
				tag = VSC
				tag = ADL
				tag = ADU
			}
			religion_group = muslim #Andalusia for Muslims
		}
		OR = {
			primary_culture = portugese
			primary_culture = galician
			primary_culture = asturian
			primary_culture = leonese
			primary_culture = extremaduran
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = lusitania_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = lusitania_group
			value = 60 #42 + (0.5 * 34) = 59 -> 60
		}
		227 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		231 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		208 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		206 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = lusitania_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = LSA	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = LSA_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_lusitania_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}	
 
# Spain	 
AN_spain_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_spain_flag }
		SPA = { exists = no }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
				tag = LSA
				tag = SPI
				tag = VSC
				tag = ADL
				tag = ADU
			}
			religion_group = muslim #Andalusia for Muslims
		}
		OR = {
			primary_culture = castillian	
			primary_culture = asturian
			primary_culture = leonese
			primary_culture = extremaduran
			primary_culture = aragonese
			primary_culture = toledan
			primary_culture = murcian
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = spain_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = spain_group
			value = 120 #96 + 20 (0.5 * 34) = 59 -> 60
		}
		217 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		219 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		1746 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		214 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = spain_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = SPA	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = SPA_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_spain_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

# Al-Andalus
AN_al_andalus_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_al_andalus_flag }
		ADL = { exists = no }
		ADU = { exists = no }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal
				tag = LSA
				tag = SPA
				tag = SPI
				tag = VSC
				tag = ADL
			}
		}
		religion_group = muslim #Al-Andalus for Muslims
		OR = {
			primary_culture = andalusi_culture
			AND = {
				culture_group = turko_semitic #Arabic
				any_owned_province = { region = iberia_region }
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = berber
				any_owned_province = { region = iberia_region }
			}
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = andalusia_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = andalusia_group
			value = 25 #10 + (0.5 * 29) = 24.5 -> 25

		224 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		225 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		1748 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		10012 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = andalusia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }

# Iberia
AN_iberia_nation = { 
	major = yes
	potential = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_iberia_flag }
		IBE = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
			} 
		}
		OR = {
			tag = LSA
			tag = SPA
			tag = SPI
			tag = VSC
			tag = ADL
			tag = ADU
			#tag = OCC
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		region = iberia_region
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		has_institution = state_sovereignty
		has_institution = nationalism_i
		adm_tech = 38 #Patriotism
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			region = iberia_region
			value = 160 
		}
		217 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		227 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		214 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		224 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }

			limit = { capital_scope = { region = iberia_region } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }

		}

		change_tag = IBE

		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = england_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = ENG	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = ENG_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_england_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

			} 
		}

			tag = FRA
			tag = ENG
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		OR = { region = british_isles_region region = france_region }
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica

			region = british_isles_region
			value = 30 #?
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { tag = ENG }
			FRA = { is_subject_of = ROOT is_subject_of_type = personal_union }
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { tag = FRA }
			ENG = { is_subject_of = ROOT is_subject_of_type = personal_union }
		}
		# ?
		236 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }

		183 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
		178 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = british_isles_region region = france_region } } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }

		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = austria_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = HAB
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = HAB_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_austria_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
			} 
		}	
		OR = { 
			tag = NGC
			tag = SGC
		}
		culture_group = germanic
	}	
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		OR = { region = north_german_region region = south_german_region }
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		has_institution = state_sovereignty
		has_institution = nationalism_i
		adm_tech = 38 #Patriotism
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			OR = { region = north_german_region region = south_german_region }
			value = 4 #
		}
		189 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { OR = { region = north_german_region region = south_german_region } } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = GER
				
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 5 } }
			set_government_rank = 5
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = GER_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_germany_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

			}

		}

				government = native 
				government = tribal 
			} 
		}
		OR = {
			tag = POL
			tag = LIT
			tag = UKR
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		OR = { province_group = poland_group province_group = lithuania_group }
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			OR = { province_group = poland_group province_group = lithuania_group }
			value = 20 #?
		}
		101 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { OR = { province_group = poland_group province_group = lithuania_group } } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = PLC	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 5 } }
			set_government_rank = 5
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = PLC_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}

			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal

				tag = GEO
				tag = KHH
				tag = CCI
				tag = VNK
				tag = LEK
				tag = AAN
				tag = AZR
			} 
		}
		OR = {
			primary_culture = circassian
			primary_culture = kabardian
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = circassia_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = circassia_group
			value = 20 #?
		}
		101 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = circassia_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = CIR	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = CIR_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_circassia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

				government = native 
				government = tribal
			}

			culture_group = armenian_group
			culture_group = byzantine_g
		}
		
		OR = {
			religion = orthodox
			religion = coptic
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = crimea_group 
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		adm_tech = 2 #Politics
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = crimea_group 
			value = 10 #14 total
		}
		101 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = crimea_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = TR1	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 3 } }
			set_government_rank = 3
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		#Name
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = armenian_group }
			overide_country_name = TAURICIA
			change_primary_culture = ghrimahayer	
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_tauricia_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = aramea_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = AME	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = AME_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_aramea_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

			value = 10 #?
		}
		101 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = hadhramaut_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }

		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = turkmenistan_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = TKM	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = TKM_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_turkmenistan_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}

				tag = MAM
				tag = PER
				tag = TIM
				tag = MUG
				tag = ARB
				tag = TAB
			} 
		}
		OR = {
			priamry_culture = gilaki
			priamry_culture = daylami
			priamry_culture = talysh
		}
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		province_group = gilan_group
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			province_group = gilan_group
			value = 20 #?
		}
		101 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { province_group = gilan_group } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }

		MTR = { exists = no }
		NOT = { 
			OR = { 
				government = native 
				government = tribal 
				tag = SIA
				tag = MSA
				tag = BOR
				tag = SUM
				tag = JAV
				tag = MMK
				tag = SVJ
			} 
		}
		priamry_culture = mazandarani
	}
	provinces_to_highlight = {
		region = indonesia_region
	}
	allow = {
		is_at_war = no
		has_institution = bureaucracy
		has_institution = printing_press
		adm_tech = 19 #Res Publica
		num_of_provinces_owned_or_owned_by_non_sovereign_subjects_with = {
			region = indonesia_region
			value = 20 #?
		}
		101 = { country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT }
	}
	effect = {
		#Integrate PUs, Domains, Fiefs
		every_subject_country = { 
			limit = { capital_scope = { region = indonesia_region } OR = { is_subject_of_type = personal_union is_subject_of_type = dominion is_subject_of_type = fief } }
			inherit = PREV
		}
		
		#Change Tag
		change_tag = MTR	
		
		#Set Govt Rank	
		if = { 
			limit = { NOT = { government_rank = 4 } }
			set_government_rank = 4
		}
		
		#Rewards
		add_prestige = 25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = centralization_modifier
			duration = 7300
		}
		
		#Change Ideas
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_custom_ideas = no
				NOT = { has_idea_group = MTR_ideas }
			}
			country_event = { id = ideagroups.1 } #Swap Ideas
		}
		
		#Disable decision
		set_country_flag = formed_mataram_flag
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
	}
	ai_importance = 400 #
}


}
